â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  function getPayloadConfigFromPayload(
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    config: ChartConfig,
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    payload: unknown,
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    key: string
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  ) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    if (typeof payload !== "object" || payload === null) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      return undefined
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    }
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const payloadPayload =
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      "payload" in payload &&
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      typeof payload.payload === "object" &&
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      payload.payload !== null
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        ? payload.payload
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        : undefined
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    let configLabelKey: string = key
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    if (
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      key in payload &&
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      typeof payload[key as keyof typeof payload] === "string"
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    ) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      configLabelKey = payload[key as keyof typeof payload] as string
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    } else if (
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      payloadPayload &&
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      key in payloadPayload &&
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      typeof payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] === "string"
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    ) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      configLabelKey = payloadPayload[
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        key as keyof typeof payloadPayload
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      ] as string
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    }

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      : config[key as keyof typeof config]
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  }

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  export function PDFPreview({ htmlContent }: PDFPreviewProps) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(5) // Updated to 5 pages
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const [zoom, setZoom] = useState(0.8)

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        setCurrentPage(currentPage - 1)

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const handleNextPage = () => {

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const handleZoomIn = () => {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      setZoom((prev) => Math.min(prev + 0.1, 2))
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    }
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    const handleZoomOut = () => {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      setZoom((prev) => Math.max(prev - 0.1, 0.3))
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    }
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚            </Button>

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚            </span>

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚            </Button>
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚          </div>

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚                transformOrigin: "top center",
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚              }}

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚          ) : (

â”‚       â”‚      }
â”‚       â”‚    | {
â”‚       â”‚        type: ActionType["DISMISS_TOAST"]
â”‚       â”‚        toastId?: ToasterToast["id"]
â”‚       â”‚      }
â”‚       â”‚    | {
â”‚       â”‚        type: ActionType["REMOVE_TOAST"]
â”‚       â”‚        toastId?: ToasterToast["id"]
â”‚       â”‚      }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  interface State {
â”‚       â”‚    toasts: ToasterToast[]
â”‚       â”‚  }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  const toastTimeouts = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>()
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  const addToRemoveQueue = (toastId: string) => {
â”‚       â”‚    if (toastTimeouts.has(toastId)) {
â”‚       â”‚      return
â”‚       â”‚    }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
â”‚       â”‚      toastTimeouts.delete(toastId)
â”‚       â”‚      dispatch({
â”‚       â”‚        type: "REMOVE_TOAST",
â”‚       â”‚        toastId: toastId,
â”‚       â”‚      })
â”‚       â”‚    }, TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY)
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    toastTimeouts.set(toastId, timeout)
â”‚       â”‚  }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  export const reducer = (state: State, action: Action): State => {
â”‚       â”‚    switch (action.type) {
â”‚       â”‚      case "ADD_TOAST":
â”‚       â”‚        return {
â”‚       â”‚          ...state,
â”‚       â”‚          toasts: [action.toast, ...state.toasts].slice(0, TOAST_LIMIT),
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚      case "UPDATE_TOAST":
â”‚       â”‚        return {
â”‚       â”‚          ...state,
â”‚       â”‚          toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
â”‚       â”‚            t.id === action.toast.id ? { ...t, ...action.toast } : t
â”‚       â”‚          ),
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚      case "DISMISS_TOAST": {
â”‚       â”‚        const { toastId } = action
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚        // ! Side effects ! - This could be extracted into a dismissToast() action,
â”‚       â”‚        // but I'll keep it here for simplicity
â”‚       â”‚        if (toastId) {
â”‚       â”‚          addToRemoveQueue(toastId)
â”‚       â”‚        } else {
â”‚       â”‚          state.toasts.forEach((toast) => {
â”‚       â”‚            addToRemoveQueue(toast.id)
â”‚       â”‚          })
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚        return {
â”‚       â”‚          ...state,
â”‚       â”‚          toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
â”‚       â”‚            t.id === toastId || toastId === undefined
â”‚       â”‚              ? {
â”‚       â”‚                  ...t,
â”‚       â”‚                  open: false,
â”‚       â”‚                }
â”‚       â”‚              : t
â”‚       â”‚          ),
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚      }
â”‚       â”‚      case "REMOVE_TOAST":
â”‚       â”‚        if (action.toastId === undefined) {
â”‚       â”‚          return {
â”‚       â”‚            ...state,
â”‚       â”‚            toasts: [],
â”‚       â”‚          }
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚        return {
â”‚       â”‚          ...state,
â”‚       â”‚          toasts: state.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.toastId),
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚    }
â”‚       â”‚  }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  const listeners: Array<(state: State) => void> = []
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  let memoryState: State = { toasts: [] }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  function dispatch(action: Action) {
â”‚       â”‚    memoryState = reducer(memoryState, action)
â”‚       â”‚    listeners.forEach((listener) => {
â”‚       â”‚      listener(memoryState)
â”‚       â”‚    })
â”‚       â”‚  }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  type Toast = Omit<ToasterToast, "id">
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  function toast({ ...props }: Toast) {
â”‚       â”‚    const id = genId()
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    const update = (props: ToasterToast) =>
â”‚       â”‚      dispatch({
â”‚       â”‚        type: "UPDATE_TOAST",
â”‚       â”‚        toast: { ...props, id },
â”‚       â”‚      })
â”‚       â”‚    const dismiss = () => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId: id })
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    dispatch({
â”‚       â”‚      type: "ADD_TOAST",
â”‚       â”‚      toast: {
â”‚       â”‚        ...props,
â”‚       â”‚        id,
â”‚       â”‚        open: true,
â”‚       â”‚        onOpenChange: (open) => {
â”‚       â”‚          if (!open) dismiss()
â”‚       â”‚        },
â”‚       â”‚      },
â”‚       â”‚    })
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    return {
â”‚       â”‚      id: id,
â”‚       â”‚      dismiss,
â”‚       â”‚      update,
â”‚       â”‚    }
â”‚       â”‚  }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  function useToast() {
â”‚       â”‚    const [state, setState] = React.useState<State>(memoryState)
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    React.useEffect(() => {
â”‚       â”‚      listeners.push(setState)
â”‚       â”‚      return () => {
â”‚       â”‚        const index = listeners.indexOf(setState)
â”‚       â”‚        if (index > -1) {
â”‚       â”‚          listeners.splice(index, 1)
â”‚       â”‚        }
â”‚       â”‚      }
â”‚       â”‚    }, [state])
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚    return {
â”‚       â”‚      ...state,
â”‚       â”‚      toast,
â”‚       â”‚      dismiss: (toastId?: string) => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId }),
â”‚       â”‚    }
â”‚       â”‚  }
â”‚       â”‚  
â”‚       â”‚  export { useToast, toast }
â”‚       â”‚

â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  // Helper function to convert image URL to base64
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  async function getImageAsBase64(url: string): Promise<string> {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    try {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      const response = await fetch(url)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      const blob = await response.blob()
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        const reader = new FileReader()
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        reader.onload = () => resolve(reader.result as string)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        reader.onerror = reject
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚        reader.readAsDataURL(blob)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      })
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    } catch (error) {
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      console.error("Failed to convert image to base64:", error)
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚      return ""
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚    }
â”‚   â”‚   â”‚  }

â”‚   â”‚  #!/usr/bin/env python3
â”‚   â”‚  """
â”‚   â”‚  Script d'analyse d'arborescence de projet
â”‚   â”‚  GÃ©nÃ¨re un fichier avec la structure complÃ¨te et le contenu des fichiers
â”‚   â”‚  """
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  import os

â”‚   â”‚  def is_text_file(filepath):
â”‚   â”‚      """DÃ©termine si un fichier est un fichier texte lisible"""
â”‚   â”‚      text_extensions = {
â”‚   â”‚          '.txt', '.md', '.py', '.js', '.ts', '.tsx', '.jsx', '.json', '.yaml', '.yml',
â”‚   â”‚          '.xml', '.html', '.htm', '.css', '.scss', '.sass', '.less', '.sql', '.sh',
â”‚   â”‚          '.bat', '.ps1', '.php', '.rb', '.java', '.c', '.cpp', '.h', '.hpp', '.cs',
â”‚   â”‚          '.go', '.rs', '.swift', '.kt', '.scala', '.clj', '.hs', '.ml', '.r', '.m',
â”‚   â”‚          '.dockerfile', '.gitignore', '.env', '.config', '.conf', '.ini', '.cfg',
â”‚   â”‚          '.toml', '.lock', '.log', '.csv', '.tsv', '.vue', '.svelte', '.astro'
â”‚   â”‚      }
â”‚   â”‚      
â”‚   â”‚      # VÃ©rification par extension
â”‚   â”‚      extension = pathlib.Path(filepath).suffix.lower()
â”‚   â”‚      if extension in text_extensions:
â”‚   â”‚          return True
â”‚   â”‚      
â”‚   â”‚      # VÃ©rification pour les fichiers sans extension (comme Dockerfile, Makefile, etc.)
â”‚   â”‚      filename = pathlib.Path(filepath).name.lower()
â”‚   â”‚      if filename in ['dockerfile', 'makefile', 'rakefile', 'license', 'readme', 'changelog', 'authors']:
â”‚   â”‚          return True
â”‚   â”‚      
â”‚   â”‚      # Test de lecture binaire pour dÃ©tecter si c'est du texte
â”‚   â”‚      try:
â”‚   â”‚          with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
â”‚   â”‚              sample = f.read(1024)
â”‚   â”‚              # Si il y a des bytes nuls, c'est probablement binaire
â”‚   â”‚              if b'\x00' in sample:
â”‚   â”‚                  return False
â”‚   â”‚              # Essayer de dÃ©coder en UTF-8
â”‚   â”‚              sample.decode('utf-8')
â”‚   â”‚              return True
â”‚   â”‚      except:
â”‚   â”‚          return False
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  def should_skip_directory(dir_name):
â”‚   â”‚      """DÃ©termine si un dossier doit Ãªtre ignorÃ©"""
â”‚   â”‚      skip_dirs = {
â”‚   â”‚          'node_modules', '.git', '.svn', '.hg', '__pycache__', '.pytest_cache',
â”‚   â”‚          'venv', 'env', '.venv', '.env', 'dist', 'build', '.next', '.nuxt',
â”‚   â”‚          'coverage', '.coverage', '.nyc_output', 'logs', 'tmp', 'temp',
â”‚   â”‚          '.DS_Store', 'Thumbs.db', '.idea', '.vscode', '.vs'
â”‚   â”‚      }
â”‚   â”‚      return dir_name in skip_dirs
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  def get_file_info(filepath):
â”‚   â”‚      """RÃ©cupÃ¨re les informations d'un fichier"""
â”‚   â”‚      try:
â”‚   â”‚          stat = os.stat(filepath)
â”‚   â”‚          size = stat.st_size
â”‚   â”‚          modified = datetime.fromtimestamp(stat.st_mtime).strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
â”‚   â”‚          return f"[{format_size(size)} - {modified}]"
â”‚   â”‚      except:
â”‚   â”‚          return "[info non disponible]"
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  def format_size(size_bytes):
â”‚   â”‚      """Formate la taille en unitÃ©s lisibles"""
â”‚   â”‚      if size_bytes < 1024:
â”‚   â”‚          return f"{size_bytes}B"
â”‚   â”‚      elif size_bytes < 1024 * 1024:
â”‚   â”‚          return f"{size_bytes/1024:.1f}KB"
â”‚   â”‚      elif size_bytes < 1024 * 1024 * 1024:
â”‚   â”‚          return f"{size_bytes/(1024*1024):.1f}MB"
â”‚   â”‚      else:
â”‚   â”‚          return f"{size_bytes/(1024*1024*1024):.1f}GB"
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  def read_file_content(filepath):
â”‚   â”‚      """Lit le contenu d'un fichier texte"""
â”‚   â”‚      try:
â”‚   â”‚          with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
â”‚   â”‚              content = f.read()
â”‚   â”‚              if len(content) > 50000:  # Limite pour Ã©viter les fichiers trop gros
â”‚   â”‚                  return content[:50000] + f"\n\n... [FICHIER TRONQUÃ‰ - Taille totale: {len(content)} caractÃ¨res] ..."
â”‚   â”‚              return content
â”‚   â”‚      except UnicodeDecodeError:
â”‚   â”‚          try:
â”‚   â”‚              with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='latin-1') as f:
â”‚   â”‚                  content = f.read()
â”‚   â”‚                  return content[:50000] + "\n\n... [FICHIER TRONQUÃ‰ - Encodage latin-1] ..." if len(content) > 50000 else content
â”‚   â”‚          except:
â”‚   â”‚              return "[ERREUR: Impossible de lire le fichier]"
â”‚   â”‚      except Exception as e:
â”‚   â”‚          return f"[ERREUR: {str(e)}]"
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  def analyze_directory(root_path, output_file, prefix="", is_last=True, parent_prefix=""):
â”‚   â”‚      """Analyse rÃ©cursivement un dossier et Ã©crit dans le fichier de sortie"""
â”‚   â”‚      
â”‚   â”‚      try:
â”‚   â”‚          items = sorted(os.listdir(root_path))
â”‚   â”‚          # SÃ©parer dossiers et fichiers
â”‚   â”‚          dirs = [item for item in items if os.path.isdir(os.path.join(root_path, item)) and not should_skip_directory(item)]
â”‚   â”‚          files = [item for item in items if os.path.isfile(os.path.join(root_path, item))]
â”‚   â”‚          
â”‚   â”‚          all_items = dirs + files
â”‚   â”‚          
â”‚   â”‚          for i, item in enumerate(all_items):
â”‚   â”‚              is_last_item = (i == len(all_items) - 1)
â”‚   â”‚              item_path = os.path.join(root_path, item)
â”‚   â”‚              
â”‚   â”‚              # Dessiner l'arborescence
â”‚   â”‚              if is_last_item:
â”‚   â”‚                  current_prefix = "â””â”€â”€ "
â”‚   â”‚                  next_prefix = parent_prefix + "    "
â”‚   â”‚              else:
â”‚   â”‚                  current_prefix = "â”œâ”€â”€ "
â”‚   â”‚                  next_prefix = parent_prefix + "â”‚   "
â”‚   â”‚              
â”‚   â”‚              if os.path.isdir(item_path):
â”‚   â”‚                  # C'est un dossier
â”‚   â”‚                  output_file.write(f"{parent_prefix}{current_prefix}ğŸ“ {item}/\n")
â”‚   â”‚                  analyze_directory(item_path, output_file, prefix + "    ", is_last_item, next_prefix)
â”‚   â”‚              else:
â”‚   â”‚                  # C'est un fichier
â”‚   â”‚                  file_info = get_file_info(item_path)
â”‚   â”‚                  output_file.write(f"{parent_prefix}{current_prefix}ğŸ“„ {item} {file_info}\n")
â”‚   â”‚                  
â”‚   â”‚                  # Lire le contenu si c'est un fichier texte
â”‚   â”‚                  if is_text_file(item_path):
â”‚   â”‚                      content = read_file_content(item_path)
â”‚   â”‚                      output_file.write(f"{next_prefix}â”Œâ”€ CONTENU:\n")
â”‚   â”‚                      
â”‚   â”‚                      # Indenter chaque ligne du contenu
â”‚   â”‚                      for line in content.split('\n'):
â”‚   â”‚                          output_file.write(f"{next_prefix}â”‚  {line}\n")
â”‚   â”‚                      
â”‚   â”‚                      output_file.write(f"{next_prefix}â””â”€ FIN DU CONTENU\n\n")
â”‚   â”‚                  else:
â”‚   â”‚                      output_file.write(f"{next_prefix}â””â”€ [FICHIER BINAIRE - Contenu non affichÃ©]\n\n")
â”‚   â”‚                      
â”‚   â”‚      except PermissionError:
â”‚   â”‚          output_file.write(f"{parent_prefix}â””â”€â”€ [ERREUR: Permission refusÃ©e]\n")
â”‚   â”‚      except Exception as e:
â”‚   â”‚          output_file.write(f"{parent_prefix}â””â”€â”€ [ERREUR: {str(e)}]\n")
â”‚   â”‚  
â”‚   â”‚  def main():
â”‚   â”‚      parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Analyse l\'arborescence d\'un projet')
â”‚   â”‚      parser.add_argument('path', nargs='?', default='.', help='Chemin du dossier Ã  analyser (dÃ©faut: dossier actuel)')
â”‚   â”‚      parser.add_argument('-o', '--output', default='project_structure.txt', help='Fichier de sortie (dÃ©faut: project_structure.txt)')
â”‚   â”‚      parser.add_argument('--no-content', action='store_true', help='Ne pas inclure le contenu des fichiers')
â”‚   â”‚      
â”‚   â”‚      args = parser.parse_args()
â”‚   â”‚      
â”‚   â”‚      root_path = os.path.abspath(args.path)
â”‚   â”‚      output_path = args.output
â”‚   â”‚
